EXPLANATION
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
This abstract lists all unique ranking expressions that appear in the
Cast Vote Record (CVR). Rankings are sorted lexicographically by candidate
order and grouped by common prefix for compression.

Format: <ranking expression> : <count>
Symbol '>' means 'preferred over'
(empty) means no ranking was cast

Prefix compression: When multiple rankings share a common prefix, the
prefix is stated once, followed by the distinct suffixes with counts.
